<div id="review_526872613" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/526872613" />
    <a title="Nicole C" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5360006-nicole-c"><img alt="Nicole C" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388549165p2/5360006.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/526872613?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole C" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole C" href="/user/show/5360006-nicole-c">Nicole C</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526872613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8186368975344140408">I thought the book was amazing! It was like your typical american teenage story but it's not. I don't know what I'm saying. I couldn't even put the book down. I loved the characteristics of each characters in the book. Especially Finn! I didn't really notice him much, but he really stood out later then. I love how strong Megan is and how she dealt with her problems in a mature way. I can see her development without her parents by her side and how she could now stand up for herself independently.</span>
  <span id="freeText8186368975344140408" style="display:none">I thought the book was amazing! It was like your typical american teenage story but it's not. I don't know what I'm saying. I couldn't even put the book down. I loved the characteristics of each characters in the book. Especially Finn! I didn't really notice him much, but he really stood out later then. I love how strong Megan is and how she dealt with her problems in a mature way. I can see her development without her parents by her side and how she could now stand up for herself independently. I also loved how she really has a genuine heart in the book. Ugh! I just love love love the book! I'm so in love with Finn. I also marked the pages of my best favorite scenes ever in the book which either made me swoon or just made me feel in awe. There should be a sequel to this book! Hopefully. I've got my fingers crossed. The ending was a cliffhanger. It didn't make sense! I'm just probably upset because I want MORE of the McGowan's boys! I also loved Doug's breakout in the book. Overall, the book was amazing. Well, at least for me. 5/5! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8186368975344140408" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ao0C1InmDhnb+ukgFOKlThriLVz4XRXhldVjdQODFPEuXCjpTjW24ovsyfYMWPlaVmOIAqcdckCU5XE/dTVgDg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('y69UQNsucGpuFwZf8JIvRQ60bCkojTZCOVyLoFi0aV2Pfn59HP3IkT4BJonoKHNRQjXJd3fNUeM4bJnqLgIdog==')})
  }

She also writes teen fiction under the name <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/62448.Kieran_Scott?from_search=true&search_version=service' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kieran Scott</a>. </span>
